<rating>5<//rating><userid>105765276421361299612< /userid>< text>
We were so excited to hear that the new and improved Mama Lupe's was now open after their remodel. Our party of 4 stopped by on a Saturday afternoon ready to have some good food and that we did! Started with two beers and some Street Corn with chips & salsa. The Street Corn was packed with fresh corn roasted just right, full of flavor, and of course lots of cotija cheese. The chips were lightly salted with plenty of crunch... totally made in house. And the salsa- yes please!! After all that we were stoked to get our meals which included an enchilada plate, quesadilla, and a grilled chicken burrito smothered in the house green sauce. EVERYTHING was delish but my favorite by far was the green sauce on the burrito. So light and flavorful with just a little bit of a spicy punch.
The remodel looks great!! You have to check out the bar top... such a personal touch that shouldn't be missed on your visit.
The ADA bathrooms are clean, crisp, and have great tile. They even have the cutest little sinks!

Can't wait to visit again soon... We will be back!!< /text>

< Text>
A computer glitch caused my goslings to be sent to my old address from a previous order eight years ago, despite the confirmation e-mail having my current address. I know this is not the norm, I have never had a problem or even heard bad things about Metzer Farms. However, this caused the birds to spend about 4.5 days in transit. My original post office forwarded them to my current address before I even knew they had been there. The people at Metzer were so incredibly nice and caring about the situation. I was impressed that they admitted their mistake quickly and apologized immediately. When I called again on Friday morning, they put a replacement in for me when we were still unable to locate the goslings. That afternoon, the post office called me and said that the birds had finally arrived and two (of three) were still alive! They were not making noise or moving much. USPS fed and watered the goslings, so by the time I received them they were standing and peeping! The roman tufted looked very shaky, but he perked up quickly! I was amazed that the female toulouse they sent was in such great shape.

I called Metzer to tell them two of the birds had survived, but they insisted on sending the full replacement order anyhow! I have to say, this was a very difficult week but the kindness and helpfulness of the people at Metzer made it a little easier to get through. I don't blame them for what was obviously a computer glitch. Instead I am impressed with their customer service and desire to make things right with customers! You can tell they run a reputable business and stand behind their name and their birds. I would definitely recommend them to anyone and plan on using them in the future for all my waterfowl (and etc...) needs!</Text>

<rate>1< /rate><text>I have been quite disappointed with the Welsh Harlequin ducks I bought from this breeder. Their genetic line has obvious mutations that are not good to perpetuate within an endangered species like the WH's (yellow bills, feathers growing on the legs, etc). I know they aren't considered "show quality", but it's bad breeding practice to continue these traits. Also, I ordered straight run ducks and was hoping to get a more even cut between males and females in my flock. I did not and I believe it is because they sexed all the ducks and filled the orders for specific male/female orders and then put the left over ducks (mainly males) into the straight-run category. Doing this is not being honest with the customer and what they ordered.

Overall, I will not be ordering from this company again and I do not recommend anyone else order from them either. Even when I called to clarify on the amount of males I received and to see if I could get a refund or some more females they were very short with me and spoke to me as if I were stupid. <user_id>113272767263478719255<//user_id>< text>
I have been quite disappointed with the Welsh Harlequin ducks I bought from this breeder. Their genetic line has obvious mutations that are not good to perpetuate within an endangered species like the WH's (yellow bills, feathers growing on the legs, etc). I know they aren't considered "show quality", but it's bad breeding practice to continue these traits. Also, I ordered straight run ducks and was hoping to get a more even cut between males and females in my flock. I did not and I believe it is because they sexed all the ducks and filled the orders for specific male/female orders and then put the left over ducks (mainly males) into the straight-run category. Doing this is not being honest with the customer and what they ordered.

Overall, I will not be ordering from this company again and I do not recommend anyone else order from them either. Even when I called to clarify on the amount of males I received and to see if I could get a refund or some more females they were very short with me and spoke to me as if I were stupid. In the future I will be looking for other breeders that are more customer oriented instead of money oriented.< /text>

< review>
Nugget is great, their chain hires the best staff. But it's a little too "speciality" items for me, so I usually only go for the health supplements, tincture type items especially Arnica. Then do my normal weekly shopping at Food 4 Less which fits MY needs but is other side of town.

But, ironically I was sent to also pick up a 2 Liter bottle of Coke. Imagine my surprise huge shelves of every imaginable soda, and the largest were 1.75L. I laughed all the way thru the checkout for my items, and stopped at a competitor on the way home for 3 for $5.<//review>
